Overview Notes: Supplement with active B vitamins such as those found in a good multivitamin (eg. Phytomulti) to bring homocysteine down to an optimal level of around 8.

Overview Notes: Supplement with active B vitamins such as those found in a good multivitamin (eg. Phytomulti) to bring homocysteine down to an optimal level of around 8.

Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: Normal clinical examination on the day.
Men's Health Recommendations: 
Women's Health Recommendations: Over the age of 40 it is recommended that you have a mammogram done. When you finish breastfeeding I would encourage you to do this.
Overview Notes: Ideally we would like the hsCRP level to fall into the low risk category for cardiovascular disease (<1). To lower inflammation follow an anti-inflammatory mediterranean style diet, decrease alcohol consumption, continue to exercise and focus on stress management. Supplements such as curcumin and omega 3's can also help.

Nurse: Lebo Cindi
Clinical Recommendations: 
Men's Health Recommendations: 
Women's Health Recommendations: Over the age of 40 it is recommended that you have a mammogram done. When you finish breastfeeding I would encourage you to do this.
Overview Notes: Ideally we would like the hsCRP level to fall into the low risk category for cardiovascular disease (<1). To lower inflammation follow an anti-inflammatory mediterranean style diet, decrease alcohol consumption, continue to exercise and focus on stress management. Supplements such as curcumin and omega 3's can also help.

To lower inflammation follow an anti-inflammatory mediterranean style diet, decrease alcohol consumption, continue to exercise and focus on stress management. Supplements such as curcumin and omega 3's can also help.

Overview Notes: Ideally we would like the hsCRP level to fall into the low risk category for cardiovascular disease (<1). To lower inflammation follow an anti-inflammatory mediterranean style diet, decrease alcohol consumption, continue to exercise and focus on stress management. Supplements such as curcumin and omega 3's can also help.
Comment Key: SymptomScreeningNote
Comment Value: None
Special Investigation Notes: Client chose not to do tests or Bio assessment

Overview Notes: Supplement with active B vitamins such as those found in a good multivitamin (eg. Phytomulti) to bring homocysteine down to an optimal level of around 8.
Comment Key: VitaminsOrSupplements
Comment Value: PregOmega
Special Investigation Notes: Client chose not to do tests or Bio assessment
